<user>107325830037888892486< /user><date>1497018693054< /date><username>Teddy S.</username><rating>4< /rating><GmapID>0x80dcd9077adfd2df:0xae13c79baa46b593<//GmapID>< text>
I thoroughly enjoyed my recent visit to La Rinconada. When I entered I was greeted warmly by the cook who took the time to explain the daily specials and went through the drink list. My fabulous server Irene took over shortly after. I told her I had just moved to the area.  She gave me some great tips on what the nightlife was like and mentioned they have live music most evenings.
For dinner I had enchiladas asada which contained crispy bits of steak smothered in salsa verde. Paired with rice and beans, it was the perfect dish.
I'll definitely be back.<//text>

Had a great time at this place. The food is great and very well priced. The owners and staff were very customer friendly. < text>
Authentic Mexican food - one of the last ones standing near downtown Santa Ana. They also have a variety of drinks and beers. They hold events and shows throughout the week and on the weekend. Parking kind of sucks in that area of Downtown Santa Ana however, once in the restaurant - it's always a great time and the owners are very welcoming and make you feel at home. You can find DJ Romeo One frequently stopping in for a drink.<//text>

<review>Went here to drop off my little brother so he could play basketball with his friends on a Friday after school.

I did not know this place offered passport services until the front desk lady mentioned it. I asked about the prices and was surprised to hear how competitive they were.

I went in the the next week to turn in the passport application. I was greeted by Brook(e) and had a flawless a-z customer service experience. By far, the best.

She explained the entire process, helped me with the paperwork when I had questions, took the photo, swore an oath (favorite part) and was done within 30-45 minutes.

I will definitely come here again in 10-15 years when my passport expires or sooner if I lose it again...

Laguna Beach Cliff Hike is a must if you're more interested in the unique often missed gems in Laguna Beach OR just want a cool run with good views :) The trail is perfect distance! Once you get higher up you will have two routes actually three if your interested exploring east. If you go the natural route to the top you have two layers of trails. Both trails are awesome once you get to the top you get a clear somewhat steep view of what appears to be The Montage golf course. Watchout for mountain lions and rattlesnakes, etc.<//Text>

<time>1519333164500<//time><rate>5<//rate><review>This is a favorite hike for our family with great views of Laguna Beach! There are two approaches and one is more difficult than the other. The south trailhead is our favorite, but is more difficult. It begins in a residential neighborhood and ascends something like 600-650 feet in a matter of a 1/4-1/2 mile. With kids, this might be a little difficult. The other approach is from the East and is much more moderate because you park on top of a hill. When you come to the fork in the trail near the end, keep right to ascend to the tallest part of the peak. The views are excellent and there is a bench at the top. Beware of the sharp cliffs with the kids!</review>< pics>
None</pics>

< text>
I went to South Coast MedSpa to get a BBL Forever Young treatment. I was a bit nervous at first, I never had it done before and had multiple doubts and concerns: what if the procedure is too invasive, what if it hurts, what if it is a wrong decision all together? However, all of my fears had disappeared after a few minutes of the initial consultation. Courtney was professional and knowledgeable, she went over the possible side effects, she explained that they prefer to start patients with milder treatments to make sure they know how the skin reacts to avoid traumatizing it too much. She also noted that milder treatments mean less dramatic results, which gave me a sense of confidence in knowing it wouldn't drastically change my appearance (that was one of my fears as well). Moreover, Megan was super nice and helpful at the front desk, addressing multiple clients by their first names, and generally seeming very involved with each one. I also had a chance to have a brief conversation with Mark, the manager, who impressed me with his enthusiasm over the treatments they offer: he seemed very excited explaining to me how they are different and what kinds of results one should expect from each one. I had a feeling he's genuinely proud of the work they do. Moreover, during the procedure itself, Courtney was supportive and encouraging, constantly informing me that I was doing good 💪, and making sure I was feeling good as well, "Is everything ok? Does this hurt?" I also need to mention that it did not hurt. I mean, some spots were more unpleasant than others, but the sensation was so brief, it's hard to call it pain, really. If I had to describe the treatment in one word, I'd say it was bright, more than anything. But that's the whole point, isn't it?
I am still waiting for the full results to show up (it takes up to 6 weeks for skin to show full rejuvenation effects after the BBL), but I already don't see some of the blood vessels that were bugging me before. Also, I did not have any redness, burning sensations, or swelling after the treatment, which I was really happy about.
I recommend this place to anyone who feels unsure, nervous, or even scared: South Coast MedSpa made me feel welcome and cared for, they listened to my concerns without judgement and answered all of the questions no matter how silly they were. There is no need to be afraid to learn more about how you can become a younger and healthier self, just schedule a consultation, so you have the information you need to make a decision.<//text>

I ate at China Wok for the very first time maybe a month ago on January 3rd. The meal I had, #56 the spicy chicken with peppers was the best I ever had. Instantly it was crowned as my new favorite Chinese restaurant. Although today 02/06/18 I came back for more and was pretty disappointed. I ordered the same meal, but this time for takeout. I wasn't in the mood to dine in since it was still comfortable weather-wise outside. So I got my food and it looked atrocious from the moment I saw it. The sauce looked liked it had been changed, there was hardly any good size chicken portions in my meal. It was skimpy, bottom of the fryer, sitting in the pan all day type chicken. The sauce made it worse. It was a waste of money. The chopped onions and peppers  were the only thing that made today's meal average at best. Advice: don't change what's not broken sauce-wise, serve fresh chicken, don't go light on portions even if it's takeout. If a dish is called chicken or etc: then it should come with a pretty adequate amount of chicken. The amount of chicken I received were the equivalent to three chicken McNuggets from McDonald's sliced into my meal. My first experience I received at least half a chicken breast of chicken. Don't like this place anymore. I'd go back, I may reconsider, but I cannot. I'm about to leave town. It's sour to me they couldn't deliver a home run combination within just one months time.</Review>

< date>
1604119112155< /date>
<rate>4< /rate>< Review>
It’s a beautiful facility which makes you feel welcome and at ease. The staff is very professional and caring and takes good care of all of us who are there to have a mammogram.
I just have two complaints: the chairs in the second waiting room (holding room just before having mammogram) are extremely low and close to the floor and people like me who have difficulty walking also have difficulty getting up from a low chair, and even though I’m short myself (5’2”). So I’m sure it’s also difficult for others!
My other complaint is the horrible robes that are given to everyone. They are heavy, hot and very uncomfortable. If you take one side off in order to have that breast X-rayed, you can hardly manage to keep the other side on due to the weight of the robe. I wish I had a lot of money, because if I did I would purchase all new robes to give the Breast Center for the comfort of all the patients who go there.</Review>

It’s a beautiful facility which makes you feel welcome and at ease. The staff is very professional and caring and takes good care of all of us who are there to have a mammogram.
I just have two complaints: the chairs in the second waiting room (holding room just before having mammogram) are extremely low and close to the floor and people like me who have difficulty walking also have difficulty getting up from a low chair, and even though I’m short myself (5’2”). Overall I really appreciate the time, care and attention to detail that memorial care provides their patients.  I had a couple procedures last summer and the radiology doctor was wonderful and kind.  This month I went back in for a follow up and the radiology doctor was not as kind or understanding as last time.  She was very casually throwing around that she does not know what my condition is and how "weird" my condition seems; even saying "she has no idea if my condition grew or not because she can't tell where it starts and stops".  This would be perfectly fine if she had spoken to me about it in a professional and educated way but it was said in a very condescending manner and like I was wasting her time.  She couldn't give me any definitive information (which is OK but leave it at that and don't throw around words like "weird" and suggest other conditions that NO OTHER doctor has every suggested to me over the last 10 years of care I've had).  As a healthcare professional  myself I found it very UNprofessional and not compassionate.  When you are dealing with any patients, ESPECIALLY patients with breast-health concerns, nonchalant and casual is not that way to go. I am HOPING she was just having a bad day because I really, really liked and trusted her last year.  I will be back and the techs are AMAZING, just disappointed.  Off to my breast surgeon and hoping for a better experience.  Overall I'm not upset that she doesn't have all the answers (that's for my breast surgeon), but this is a very sensitive topic and it's my health that I'm trying to keep up with. If you are not in a rush (it took us about 2 hours to get our dinners) and are used to the slow service in Crescent city than this is your place. Understaffed and overworked the restraunt was clearly in need of a manager to take control of the place and get the food and drinks out in a reasonable amount of time (it took easily 20 minutes every time we ordered a drink). The food itself was ok, the oysters were cleaned properly but tasted not the freshest, the Ahi tuna was overly peppered for my taste (too spicy), the rib eye a thin cut for 25$, and the philly was good.< /text>
